Sir,
With reference to the aforeaaid context, we hereby submit as followai
1, In our earlier representation made to you on 12.6,97 we have inter-
alia submitted to you that Section ^ of the U.P, Special Area Development
Authorities Act, 1986 is void as tne same ia ultravlres the power of tbe
State Legislature under Article 246 of the Constitution of India, Therefore
the State Government has no Juirisdiction or power to impose the said cess
by enacting Shaktinagar Special Area Develt^ment Authority (Cess on Mineral
Rii^hts) Rules, 1997. In view of this it was submitted that we are not
liable to deposit or pay the said cess,
?
 • 
:
2, In the notice under reference you have directed ^1 the consuBers
drawing coal from you by road to deposit tbe impugnedoess alongwith sales
tax thereon before liftiivi; of coal, It is submitted that since the basic
notification levying the impngned cess issued by the State Government and
alleged to have been published on 24.2,97, le itself ultra-vires the powers
of the State Legislature undsr Article 246 of the constitution of India,
therefore the notice dated ?,6,97 issued by you based on the said impugned
notification does not have any force of law and therefore tbe sane is
and void ab-initio. We are not legally bound to comply with the same.
3, '^thout prejudice to the above, it is further submitted that tbe 
ii'
threat in the form of condition given in the said notice that "for fresh ;
release from 3,6,97 consumers desirous to draw coal from above projects
will deposit the SSADA CiSSS alongwith ooal value falling which their
application will not be oonsidered.
is illegal and unconstitutional.
You can not take undue advantage of your being in the monopoly position
by Imposing such illegal conditions on supply of coal to us. You can not
force us to deposit tbe illegal oess alongwith the sales tax C® 256) tbereun
by threatening to reject our application for supply of coal on the ground
of nott-depositing Ms illegal levy. Any rejeotion of the application for
supply of coal by you on the ground of non depositing of tbe impugned cess
would be arbitrary, illegal and oi.>ntrary to rule of law.
i {ff?
i .r
HINDALGO INDUSTRIES LTD.
jti i'
4. 
Without prejudice to the oontentloa that the Impugned levy
Itself Is without jurisdiction and illegal, it is further submitted
that this notice dated 7*6»^>7 is surbitraxy and disorlminatoxy as
it would be applicable only to those consumers who drive coal from
KCL ly road. It necessarily follows that the consumers drawing
coal through other modes of transport would not have to pay the
impugned cess at the rates given in the notice.
5. It is submitted that our business is getting adversely affected
because of you illegal demands and unauthorised notices issued in
gross violation of Article 14 and 19(l)Cg) of the Constitution of
India. 
I
In view of the above submissions, we hereby request you to withdraw
forthwith the said noticet dated 7.6,97 and accordingly issue
necessary direction or order or notice.
Thanking you.
Yours faithfully.

persons holding miAlng leases for ooal/stone/sand(or biying coal from
them) are only liable for payment of tbe cess. Tbe impugned cess is
not payable by any other person having any right or interest in the
land or in other words the cess is not payable by laod holders in
general but only by holders of mining leases within the area. 
The
subject matter of the impugned cess therefore is the mineral raised
from tbe land held in connection with mineral rights. If no mi erals
are raised, tbe cess is not leviable. The cess Is not dependent on
tne extent of land held and/or the value of land but the liability to
pay cess is dependent on the quantity of the minerals raised from
the land.

enactment you have no jurindiotion to impose any levy on mineral rights.
